    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer4749641204838935188">This was an exceptional read. The story begins on July 5, 2018, when a federal convicted felon kills an U.S. marshal while escaping and comes to an explosive ending on September 29, 2020, two months from today. Pack’s Posse, led by U.S. Marshal Simon Pack, retired marine corp general, West Point Commandant, and ex-governor set a record for bringing felons to justice while butting heads with U.S. Martial Service’s director. The stories within this story read like the best of the true crimes genre</span>
  <span id="freeText4749641204838935188" style="display:none">This was an exceptional read. The story begins on July 5, 2018, when a federal convicted felon kills an U.S. marshal while escaping and comes to an explosive ending on September 29, 2020, two months from today. Pack’s Posse, led by U.S. Marshal Simon Pack, retired marine corp general, West Point Commandant, and ex-governor set a record for bringing felons to justice while butting heads with U.S. Martial Service’s director. The stories within this story read like the best of the true crimes genre and keeps the reader turning the pages. The characters that Vermillion has created are so lifelike, the dialogue so realistic, that I felt as if I knew these people. What happens to Pack well, you must read this book to find that out… makes him seem all that much more real.<br /><br /> Vermillion is the new master of the crime thriller genre.</span>

<div id="review_3595363430" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Pegboard" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47722544-pegboard"><img alt="Pegboard" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498516338p2/47722544.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3595363430?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3595363430" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18386875900465646271">Pack's Posse by John M Vermillion is the eighth book in the Simon Pack series and they seem to get better each time. As a US Marshal, Pack faces not only the deadliest criminals, but now he has to watch his back from a jealous superior. His task force supports him with their loyalty as he has proven he would lay down his life for them. There are parts of this novel that really hit a nerve, because of where our country is right now. This novel feels like it was lived out.<br/><br/>With a strong moral compa</span>
  <span id="freeText18386875900465646271" style="display:none">Pack's Posse by John M Vermillion is the eighth book in the Simon Pack series and they seem to get better each time. As a US Marshal, Pack faces not only the deadliest criminals, but now he has to watch his back from a jealous superior. His task force supports him with their loyalty as he has proven he would lay down his life for them. There are parts of this novel that really hit a nerve, because of where our country is right now. This novel feels like it was lived out.<br /><br />With a strong moral compass and excellent leadership skills, Simon Pack leads his team in an action pack novel to hunt down the killers. John M Vermillion is an impressive author. Pack's Posse quickly draws the reader in with the kidnapping and killing of a family to start this thriller off and it only gets more intense from there. Overall, this novel is extreme, powerful, and a multi-layered crime story. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18386875900465646271" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Re/D4HEqlGdVAfo7CbGV7Ar23UPbJ07jR7YvPPhp2Sc6dSH8aLuPj16bMCMSSFSORDWOoBysa4qDUjp289+Dow==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mPq68HeMEYMmHyvjpIQ2ajQE/8zbXn+dbSAF2MgbkEXnYFjsbh0Kay2F4fu/ffcIesesLxzVWvSpxBCSw63KwQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4318914745086814736">19 Nov 20: "Packfire" is now available in print and Kindle versions. I always appreciate your reviews. <br/><br/>Still haven't decided whether I will continue the Simon Pack series. Writing Pack's story has brought me great pleasure, so much pleasure that if I pick up new settings and characters, I'll almost assuredly return to Pack at some point.<br/><br/>In 1992 I was at a dinner party at the Kuwait home of a Briti</span>
  <span id="freeText4318914745086814736" style="display:none">19 Nov 20: "Packfire" is now available in print and Kindle versions. I always appreciate your reviews. <br /><br />Still haven't decided whether I will continue the Simon Pack series. Writing Pack's story has brought me great pleasure, so much pleasure that if I pick up new settings and characters, I'll almost assuredly return to Pack at some point.<br /><br />In 1992 I was at a dinner party at the Kuwait home of a British Brigadier. The other dozen or so around the table were all from the UK. A lady seated beside me was saying something about American movies. I was listening to her when out of the ether came a random thought, which was..."if I ever write a novel, my main character's name will be Simon Pack." I never had cause to relate that to anyone until I actually wrote my first novel, "The Supe: A Novel of West Point."<br /><br /><br />I graduated from the US Military Academy at West Point and retired from the US Army as an Infantry Colonel. After active duty I worked overseas (Germany, Kuwait, Saudi Arabia, Croatia, Bosnia, and Iraq) in a variety of military-like positions. I completed numerous military programs, including the Airborne and Ranger programs, and also graduated from the School of Advanced Military Studies and the National War College. I served in combat, and have earned three Masters' Degrees. <br /><br />I love all things outdoors, and have a special connection to Montana, to which I make an annual pilgrimage. More generally, I love the Mountain West. Even more generally, I love our nation, each region of which holds its individual charms and spectactular vistas. <br /><br />In assessing fiction, I ask the three fundamental questions: (1) what did the author say? (2) how well did he say it?, and (3) was it worth saying to begin with? In my opinion, too many novelists pay too little attention to the last question. With that in mind, I try to write only about matters I believe ought to be relevant and important to people, American citizens principally.<br /><br />I love rural settings, so if you're looking for a novel set in New York City or LA, look elsewhere. With respect to characters, I want humble men and women who stress themselves physically and intellectually, people striving to be lifetime learners, people uncomfortable with too much comfort and relaxation, and people whose examples will strengthen the character of their followers.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4318914745086814736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
